              </li>

                10 Wildly Colorful Kitchens That Thrill and Delight
                <img src="http://st.houzz.com/fimgs/e03142280f904adc_0980-w214-h160-b0-p0--contemporary-kitchen.jpg" style="display:none;"/>

                No Neutral Ground? Why the Color Camps Are So Opinionated

          <h1 class="large-header mbl top" id="galleryTitleDisplay" itemprop="headline">
           What Goes With Red Walls?
          </h1>
         </div>
         <h2 class="small-header top" id="gallerySubtitleDisplay" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
          These coordinating colors and materials will make your red walls look right at home
         </h2>
         <meta content="http://st.houzz.com/simgs/1501f3da0106edc9_3-3666/modern-living-room.jpg" itemprop="image"/>
        </div>

        <div class="viewGalleryDescriptionHolder" itemprop="description">
         <div class="viewGalleryDescription " id="viewGalleryDescription">
          Red walls can be bold, vivacious, classic  and hard to decorate around! If you loved the
          <i>
           idea
          </i>
          of red walls when you painted them but now feel at a loss for what else to put in the room, these decorating ideas are here to help.
         </div>
        </div>
        <div class="out" id="gallerySpaces" itemprop="articleBody" lb-context="gallery_28610005" scopeid="gallerySpaces">
         <div class="gallery-photo-container landscape " lb-sid="5171787" objid="5171787" posid="0">
          <div class="gallery-photo reloadMe trackMe" data-full="746,503" data-stnd="606,409">
           <a compid="img" href="http://www.houzz.com/photos/5171787/Manhattan-Upper-West-Side-Vogue-Brasil-eclectic-living-room-new-york">
            <div>
             <img alt="Eclectic Living Room by Jacob Snavely Photography" class="hide-context reloadable" data-pin-no-hover="true" height="409" lb-mag="" lb-view="" oncontextmenu="PhotoContextMenu.show(event,'5171787');return false;" ondragstart="return false" onmousedown="preventImageDrag(event)" onselectstart="return false" src="http://st.houzz.com/fimgs/9011aa0b0207ec2c_3119-w606-h409-b0-p0--eclectic-living-room.jpg" width="606"/>
            </div>
           </a>
           <div class="space-link tiny-text" compid="more">
            <a href="http://www.houzz.com/photos/5171787/Manhattan-Upper-West-Side-Vogue-Brasil-eclectic-living-room-new-york">
             <span class="more-icon">
             </span>
            </a>
           </div>
           <div class="gallery-photo-credit tiny-text" compid="credit">
            <a class="hz-username" href="http://www.houzz.com/pro/jacobsnavely/jacob-snavely-photography">
             <span class="pro-name">
              Jacob Snavely Photography
             </span>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="gallery-text">
           <div class="thBuzz" hid="5171787">
            <b>
             Gallery wall.
            </b>
            Red walls create a striking backdrop for an eclectic collection of artwork. This is also a great way to tone down the red a bit
            <span>
            </span>
            <span>
              the frames will cover up some of the surface area, leaving just enough red exposed to be exciting without overwhelming your space.
            </span>
            <br/>
            <br/>
            <b>
             Black and white.
            </b>
            What will go with your red art wall? Try white upholstered furniture, a crisp black and white rug, and simple white curtains. Tie in the wall color by choosing toss pillows covered in interesting textiles with a bit of red in them
            <span>
            </span>
            <span>
              perhaps made from pieces of an old kilim rug or sari silk.
             <br/>
            </span>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="gallery-photo-container landscape " lb-sid="590353" objid="590353" posid="1">
          <div class="gallery-photo reloadMe trackMe" data-full="746,496" data-stnd="606,403">
           <a compid="img" href="http://www.houzz.com/photos/590353/Contemporary-Dining-Room-contemporary-dining-room-denver">
            <div>
             <img alt="Contemporary Dining Room Contemporary Dining Room" class="hide-context reloadable" data-pin-no-hover="true" height="403" lb-mag="" lb-view="" oncontextmenu="PhotoContextMenu.show(event,'590353');return false;" ondragstart="return false" onmousedown="preventImageDrag(event)" onselectstart="return false" src="http://st.houzz.com/fimgs/f9a1ef360f4281e8_6231-w606-h403-b0-p0--contemporary-dining-room.jpg" width="606"/>
            </div>
           </a>
          </div>
          <div class="gallery-text">
           <div class="thBuzz" hid="590353">
            <b>
             White and blue.
            </b>
            Red, white and blue can read as all-American or a nod to the French
            <span>
            </span>
            <span>
             
            </span>
            either way, this color combo is undeniably chic. Take a cue from the dining space shown here and pair a modern light fixture and chairs in white with red walls and blue cushions.
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="gallery-photo-container portrait " lb-sid="46599" objid="46599" posid="2">
          <div class="gallery-photo trackMe">
           <a compid="img" href="http://www.houzz.com/photos/46599/Dining-Room-contemporary-dining-room-san-francisco">
            <div>
             <img alt="Contemporary Dining Room by Glenn Robert Lym Architect" class="hide-context " data-pin-no-hover="true" height="632" lb-mag="" lb-view="" oncontextmenu="PhotoContextMenu.show(event,'46599');return false;" ondragstart="return false" onmousedown="preventImageDrag(event)" onselectstart="return false" src="http://st.houzz.com/fimgs/b0f1c8220ba08dd0_5404-w422-h632-b0-p0--contemporary-dining-room.jpg" width="422"/>
            </div>
           </a>
           <div class="space-link tiny-text" compid="more">
            <a href="http://www.houzz.com/photos/46599/Dining-Room-contemporary-dining-room-san-francisco">
             <span class="more-icon">
             </span>
            </a>
           </div>
           <div class="gallery-photo-credit tiny-text" compid="credit">
            <a class="hz-username" href="http://www.houzz.com/pro/lymarch/glenn-robert-lym-architect">
             <span class="pro-name">
              Glenn Robert Lym Architect
             </span>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="gallery-text">
           <div class="thBuzz" hid="46599">
            For a more relaxed take on the red, white and blue scheme, add a weathered farm table, simple wicker chairs
            <span>
             and a plate rack filled with blue and white dishes.
             <br/>
             <br/>
            </span>
            <b>
             Design dilemma: accent wall or all red?
            </b>
            As a rule of thumb, large rooms, open floor plans and kids spaces can benefit from a little more white space. Define a nook or an alcove with red paint and leave the rest crisp white. Small, cozy dining rooms and studies are better able to handle four walls of red.
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="gallery-photo-container portrait " lb-sid="569157" objid="569157" posid="3">
          <div class="gallery-photo trackMe">
           <a compid="img" href="http://www.houzz.com/photos/569157/San-Rafael-Villa-eclectic-home-theater-san-francisco">
            <div>
             <img alt="Eclectic Home Theater by Jane Ellison" class="hide-context " data-pin-no-hover="true" height="634" lb-mag="" lb-view="" oncontextmenu="PhotoContextMenu.show(event,'569157');return false;" ondragstart="return false" onmousedown="preventImageDrag(event)" onselectstart="return false" src="http://st.houzz.com/fimgs/0221a01e0f39bdaa_8810-w422-h634-b0-p0--eclectic-home-theater.jpg" width="422"/>
            </div>
           </a>
           <div class="space-link tiny-text" compid="more">
            <a href="http://www.houzz.com/photos/569157/San-Rafael-Villa-eclectic-home-theater-san-francisco">
             <span class="more-icon">
             </span>
            </a>
           </div>
           <div class="gallery-photo-credit tiny-text" compid="credit">
            <a class="hz-username" href="http://www.houzz.com/pro/4537/jane-ellison">
             <span class="pro-name">
              Jane Ellison
             </span>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="gallery-text">
           <div class="thBuzz" hid="569157">
            <b>
             Beige and orange.
            </b>
            When a comfortable, cozy look is what you want, turn to natural shades of orange (with a little brown in them), beige and off-white. Pair these warm tones with rich red walls and natural fibers.
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="gallery-photo-container portrait " lb-sid="368797" objid="368797" posid="4">
          <div class="gallery-photo trackMe">
           <a compid="img" href="http://www.houzz.com/photos/368797/reading-room-rustic-hall-phoenix">
            <div>
             <img alt="Rustic Hall by Don Ziebell" class="hide-context " data-pin-no-hover="true" height="518" lb-mag="" lb-view="" oncontextmenu="PhotoContextMenu.show(event,'368797');return false;" ondragstart="return false" onmousedown="preventImageDrag(event)" onselectstart="return false" src="http://st.houzz.com/fimgs/6b418d6b0ec57663_4245-w422-h518-b0-p0--rustic-hall.jpg" width="422"/>
            </div>
           </a>
           <div class="space-link tiny-text" compid="more">
            <a href="http://www.houzz.com/photos/368797/reading-room-rustic-hall-phoenix">
             <span class="more-icon">
             </span>
            </a>
           </div>
           <div class="gallery-photo-credit tiny-text" compid="credit">
            <a class="hz-username" href="http://www.houzz.com/pro/dzozaz/don-ziebell">
             <span class="pro-name">
              Don Ziebell
             </span>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="gallery-text">
           <div class="thBuzz" hid="368797">
            <b>
             Natural wood, leather and iron.
            </b>
            Hunky wooden beams, iron light fixtures, leather upholstery and cranberry walls strike a pleasing balance between rustic and refined. Straight white would have looked too pristine next to this rich mix of textures.
            <span>
             If you want to use white paint on trim or in an adjoining room,
            </span>
            <span>
             try parchment or linen white instead.
            </span>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="gallery-photo-container landscape " lb-sid="46348" objid="46348" posid="5">
          <div class="gallery-photo reloadMe trackMe" data-full="746,589" data-stnd="606,479">
           <a compid="img" href="http://www.houzz.com/photos/46348/Old-Farmhouse-traditional-kitchen-san-francisco">
            <div>
             <img alt="Traditional Kitchen by Mahoney Architects &amp; Interiors" class="hide-context reloadable" data-pin-no-hover="true" height="479" lb-mag="" lb-view="" oncontextmenu="PhotoContextMenu.show(event,'46348');return false;" ondragstart="return false" onmousedown="preventImageDrag(event)" onselectstart="return false" src="http://st.houzz.com/fimgs/1cb1915a0b9e7b07_1000-w606-h479-b0-p0--traditional-kitchen.jpg" width="606"/>
            </div>
           </a>
           <div class="space-link tiny-text" compid="more">
            <a href="http://www.houzz.com/photos/46348/Old-Farmhouse-traditional-kitchen-san-francisco">
             <span class="more-icon">
             </span>
            </a>
           </div>
           <div class="gallery-photo-credit tiny-text" compid="credit">
            <a class="hz-username" href="http://www.houzz.com/pro/greenbydesign/mahoney-architects-and-interiors">
             <span class="pro-name">
              Mahoney Architects &amp; Interiors
             </span>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="gallery-text">
           <div class="thBuzz" hid="46348">
            <b>
             Marble and cream.
            </b>
            Red walls in the kitchen are unexpected
            <span>
              and have the potential to be utterly gorgeous.
            </span>
            <span>
             <span>
             </span>
             Try them with marble counters, cream cabinets and wood floors for a fancy take on the farmhouse look. Looking to save? A marble-topped island is a more affordable way to include this luxurious material without breaking the bank.
             <br/>
            </span>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="gallery-photo-container landscape " lb-sid="522783" objid="522783" posid="6">
          <div class="gallery-photo reloadMe trackMe" data-full="746,657" data-stnd="606,534">
           <a compid="img" href="http://www.houzz.com/photos/522783/Lullwater-eclectic-living-room-other-metro">
            <div>
             <img alt="Eclectic Living Room by Dillard Pierce Design Associates" class="hide-context reloadable" data-pin-no-hover="true" height="534" lb-mag="" lb-view="" oncontextmenu="PhotoContextMenu.show(event,'522783');return false;" ondragstart="return false" onmousedown="preventImageDrag(event)" onselectstart="return false" src="http://st.houzz.com/fimgs/ca91cb8f0f280a15_4723-w606-h534-b0-p0--eclectic-living-room.jpg" width="606"/>
            </div>
           </a>
           <div class="space-link tiny-text" compid="more">
            <a href="http://www.houzz.com/photos/522783/Lullwater-eclectic-living-room-other-metro">
             <span class="more-icon">
             </span>
            </a>
           </div>
           <div class="gallery-photo-credit tiny-text" compid="credit">
            <a class="hz-username" href="http://www.houzz.com/pro/dillardpierce/dillard-pierce-design-associates">
             <span class="pro-name">
              Dillard Pierce Design Associates
             </span>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="gallery-text">
           <div class="thBuzz" hid="522783">
            <b>
             Oriental or kilim rug.
            </b>
            These rugs tend to include red, making them a natural choice for a room with painted red walls. Roll out a plush Oriental rug or flat-weave kilim in shades of red and blue or brown, and your red walls will instantly feel more settled in.
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="gallery-photo-container landscape " lb-sid="2624267" objid="2624267" posid="7">
          <div class="gallery-photo reloadMe trackMe" data-full="746,494" data-stnd="606,401">
           <a compid="img" href="http://www.houzz.com/photos/2624267/Atomic-Ranch-Renovation-modern-living-room-atlanta">
            <div>
             <img alt="Modern Living Room by Brian Patterson Designs, Inc." class="hide-context reloadable" data-pin-no-hover="true" height="401" lb-mag="" lb-view="" oncontextmenu="PhotoContextMenu.show(event,'2624267');return false;" ondragstart="return false" onmousedown="preventImageDrag(event)" onselectstart="return false" src="http://st.houzz.com/fimgs/1501f3da0106edc9_3666-w606-h401-b0-p0--modern-living-room.jpg" width="606"/>
            </div>
           </a>
           <div class="space-link tiny-text" compid="more">
            <a href="http://www.houzz.com/photos/2624267/Atomic-Ranch-Renovation-modern-living-room-atlanta">
             <span class="more-icon">
             </span>
            </a>
           </div>
           <div class="gallery-photo-credit tiny-text" compid="credit">
            <a class="hz-username" href="http://www.houzz.com/pro/brianpattersondesigns/brian-patterson-designs-inc">
             <span class="pro-name">
              Brian Patterson Designs, Inc.
             </span>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="gallery-text">
           <div class="thBuzz" hid="2624267">
            <b>
             Wild card: hot pink and navy.
            </b>
            If you like bold colors, push the envelope a bit by pairing red walls with hot pink and navy blue furniture. Like the opulent hues of an Indian sari, red, pink and navy make a vivacious combination.
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="gallery-photo-container landscape " lb-sid="1506789" objid="1506789" posid="8">
          <div class="gallery-photo reloadMe trackMe" data-full="746,496" data-stnd="606,403">
           <a compid="img" href="http://www.houzz.com/photos/1506789/Hampton-lane-mediterranean-dining-room-san-diego">
            <div>
             <img alt="Mediterranean Dining Room by Studio V Interior Design" class="hide-context reloadable" data-pin-no-hover="true" height="403" lb-mag="" lb-view="" oncontextmenu="PhotoContextMenu.show(event,'1506789');return false;" ondragstart="return false" onmousedown="preventImageDrag(event)" onselectstart="return false" src="http://st.houzz.com/fimgs/f0f1a3f700412d06_8649-w606-h403-b0-p0--mediterranean-dining-room.jpg" width="606"/>
            </div>
           </a>
           <div class="space-link tiny-text" compid="more">
            <a href="http://www.houzz.com/photos/1506789/Hampton-lane-mediterranean-dining-room-san-diego">
             <span class="more-icon">
             </span>
            </a>
           </div>
           <div class="gallery-photo-credit tiny-text" compid="credit">
            <a class="hz-username" href="http://www.houzz.com/pro/veronicav/studio-v-interior-design">
             <span class="pro-name">
              Studio V Interior Design
             </span>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="gallery-text">
           <div class="thBuzz" hid="1506789">
            <b>
             Dark wood and tile floors.
            </b>
            Red walls look classic and refined with warm-toned tile floors and dark wood furniture. Add layers of visual interest with a statement pendant light, a carved wood mirror and lush potted trees.
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="gallery-photo-container landscape " lb-sid="1283596" objid="1283596" posid="9">
          <div class="gallery-photo reloadMe trackMe" data-full="746,729" data-stnd="606,592">
           <a compid="img" href="http://www.houzz.com/photos/1283596/Calabasas-Spanish-Colonial-Home-mediterranean-dining-room-los-angeles">
            <div>
             <img alt="Mediterranean Dining Room by Blackband Design" class="hide-context reloadable" data-pin-no-hover="true" height="592" lb-mag="" lb-view="" oncontextmenu="PhotoContextMenu.show(event,'1283596');return false;" ondragstart="return false" onmousedown="preventImageDrag(event)" onselectstart="return false" src="http://st.houzz.com/fimgs/878111f20016d385_6098-w606-h592-b0-p0--mediterranean-dining-room.jpg" width="606"/>
            </div>
           </a>
           <div class="space-link tiny-text" compid="more">
            <a href="http://www.houzz.com/photos/1283596/Calabasas-Spanish-Colonial-Home-mediterranean-dining-room-los-angeles">
             <span class="more-icon">
             </span>
            </a>
           </div>
           <div class="gallery-photo-credit tiny-text" compid="credit">
            <a class="hz-username" href="http://www.houzz.com/pro/blackband/blackband-design">
             <span class="pro-name">
              Blackband Design
             </span>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="gallery-text">
           <div class="thBuzz" hid="1283596">
            Blue end chairs and printed curtains temper the warmth of the red walls, rug and tile floors here. This is also good inspiration for changing the look of your space down the road, simply by adding new seat cushions and window treatments.
            <span>
             <br/>
            </span>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="gallery-photo-container portrait " lb-sid="872020" objid="872020" posid="10">
          <div class="gallery-photo trackMe">
           <a compid="img" href="http://www.houzz.com/photos/872020/Red-Study-traditional-living-room-san-francisco">
            <div>
             <img alt="Traditional Living Room by Bashford Design" class="hide-context " data-pin-no-hover="true" height="632" lb-mag="" lb-view="" oncontextmenu="PhotoContextMenu.show(event,'872020');return false;" ondragstart="return false" onmousedown="preventImageDrag(event)" onselectstart="return false" src="http://st.houzz.com/fimgs/d5b105cd0fa02343_4537-w422-h632-b0-p0--traditional-living-room.jpg" width="422"/>
            </div>
           </a>
           <div class="space-link tiny-text" compid="more">
            <a href="http://www.houzz.com/photos/872020/Red-Study-traditional-living-room-san-francisco">
             <span class="more-icon">
             </span>
            </a>
           </div>
           <div class="gallery-photo-credit tiny-text" compid="credit">
            <a class="hz-username" href="http://www.houzz.com/pro/bashfordanddale/bashford-design">
             <span class="pro-name">
              Bashford Design
             </span>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="gallery-text">
           <div class="thBuzz" hid="872020">
            <b>
             Chocolate, black and gold.
            </b>
            Try a plush chocolate-colored sofa, lamps with black parchment shades, and picture frames and mirrors in either black or gold (or a mix). On the floor you could go with either a traditional rug in red tones (as seen here) or keep it simple with a natural-fiber rug.
            <br/>
            <br/>
            <b>
             Tell us:
            </b>
            Do you have red walls? How do you decorate around them? Share your photos and tips in the Comments!
            <br/>
            <br/>
            <b>
             More:
            </b>
            <a href="http://www.houzz.com/ideabooks/red" target="_blank">
             Houzz guides to working with red
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>

               Linus! That is where you made your mistake. You don't want to MATCH the red! It is the color that accompanies the others. Red looks good with as a partner with so many other colors. Red, black and white......red , chocolate and gold,,,,,red, silver and gray.....red, cream and navy.....red, blue and brown. And of course,depending on the shade of red, the possibilities grow tenfold. Be creative! Don't match! Pair!

              <span class="hz-username hzHouzzer hzHCUserName " data-id="ahp325" data-type="profile">
               ahp325
              </span>
              <div class="commentBodyText">
               I adore red, with brown leather and dark wood furniture, perhaps pops of cream,blue,yellow, even olive greens beiges and metallics, a couple of green plants it can be so warm, cozy, and stunning! In a kitchen with creamy cabinets, positively delicious. I find the earthy/muted reds much easier to work with. It's all in how much you use and how you accent it. I suspect people who have an aversion to red are probably drawn to cooler tones as a rule. I look good in red and sickly in baby blue, any pastel really.But you see light blue EVERYWHERE especially anywhere near a beach. I love them in other people houses, but not mine. When you're in your private sanctuary should you should be surrounded by colors you adore and that adore you back :)
              </div>

              <span class="hz-username hzHouzzer hzHCUserName " data-id="stellans" data-type="profile">
               Nancy Sloop
              </span>
              <div class="commentBodyText">
               Our connected-with-divided-knee-walls-entry living room and dining room had wainscoting all around except for the windows wall, and we painted the other walls a matte light gray (Sherwin-Williams The Big Chill) and wainscoting was white. What to do with the 3-window wall both rooms had in common? We felt another gray or white while might make the rooms too boring, and my DH was really wanting some strong color somewhere... so we went with a matte red wall (Sherwin-Williams Bolero). We are delighted with how it turned out. We have an old family rug in the living room over dark hardwood floors.
              </div>

              <div class="commentBodyText">
               I love red walls (and all warm colors in general).  My dining room has one red wall where a piece of statement art hangs.  Other walls are a warm, slightly orangey yellow.  The painting is in reds, yellows and black.  There is lots of natural light during the day so it never feels claustrophobic and at night, with the chandelier lit,  it glows.  I also have a large bedroom with all red walls.  It has dark wood furniture, ivory trim and plantation shutters, an oriental rug and a tapestry-like coverlet over ivory bedding.  It has a bit of a British Colonial vibe.  I need to add a couple of large plants.

        if (HZ.data &amp;&amp; HZ.data.Spaces) {
            var space = HZ.data.Spaces.get(spaceId);
            if (space) {
                HZ.dialogs.EmailDialog.prepare({
                    type: HZ.sendEmail.types.SPACE,
                    referenceId: space.id,
                    subject: space.t,
                    message: (space.prod ? HZ.sendEmail.texts.DEFAULT_MESSAGE_PRODUCT : HZ.sendEmail.texts.DEFAULT_MESSAGE_SPACE)
                });
                HZ.ui.Yamdi.show (HZ.dialogs.EmailDialog);
            }
        }
    }
	function showSendEmailDialogWithMessage (message) {
		HZ.dialogs.EmailDialog.prepare({
			type: 1,
			referenceId: 28610005,
			subject: "What Goes With Red Walls?",
			message: message
		});
		HZ.ui.Yamdi.show (HZ.dialogs.EmailDialog);
	}

	function showSendEmailDialog () {
		showSendEmailDialogWithMessage("Take a look at these great spaces that I found on Houzz, and let me know what you think.");
	}

		function setUrl_(e){
			url = detokenize(click_data_obj_[e.getAttribute('sid')]);
			e.href = url;
		}		
		
		function detokenize(data) {
			return data[0] + "=" + data[2] + data[1];
		}
